natt riche men heuyn techyth howe ye may entre yates heuyn sayth gospel yate weye ledith lyf blysse fulle strayte fewe passe therby soo nedyl vnderstonde entre heuyns blysse camel chargyd riche men doiste many men doon thou allegyst scripture lyste applyest thy fantasye leuyst behynd liste whiche ayenste thy fantasye hole prayer salomon mendicitatem et diuicias ne dede ri michi tribue tantum victui meo necessaria ne forte saciatus illiciar ad negandum et dicam quis est domin et egestate co pulsus furer et periurem nom dei mei beggerye sayth rich ne yeue thou nat yeue thou lyuelode ne foryet god endles godes also syde vnpacience pouert compelle nat stele neither forswere whiche prayer refusith pouertie thanne dothe aboundaunce richesse prayer differently biholdith grete richesse moche pouertie also sir sauf thy pacience thou rehersist wordes salomones pyer false englisshe nat conuenyent saide nat yeue neither richesse ne beggerye thou saydest sayde yeue richesse beggery saye therof kepith theym straungere whiche shal deuoure al gettyth moche care ayen myscheyf beggery couetyse salomon made prayer sayenge lorde yeue nat richesse beggerye gyder suche nygarshyp beggerye kynge sayde ego autem mendicus sum et pauper sayd begger pore man glose saith th beggynge axe thynge nother hath self riche man nedythe thane pore axe help shewyd afore ergo nedith beg thane pore man oure gylte oure synne oure sake shulde neuir elles haue sworne goddes deth ne wepte salte terys eyn oure gylt nat owne shulde neuir elles haue sworne goddes iyen ne hadde stuge herte shedde precio body ne bone ne blode ayest endlesse loue yt shewyd v shewe hi grete vnkyndnes ayest grete worship yt v brought v endles worship ouir grete velony pwe fynde miracle lady sumtym ther iustice rightful many soules flaterig tunge worste al therfore wyse man sayth susurro et bilignis erit maledictus deo ecle xxviii musterer double tungedman shal accursed god troubleth moche folke haue pe thyrde thunge sayth hath stired moued moch peple oute pee disparlid theym fronacion nacion fourthe chapter diues susurro yt cleped musterer pau preuey towner pryuely telleth false tale mongis people make discencion debate mongis people telle tale preuely whyche dare tel opely ne may vowe whych folke saint poule saythe susurrones detractores deo odibiles ad ro ic musterers bacbyters god hateth susurro preuy bacbiter preuy lyer maketh debate amo ge frendes wyse man sayth god hateth al tho sowen discord mongis bretherne frendes uer vic sayth nother place preuy musterers defoule ther soule thei shalbe hated ol bothe god al courte heuen eccle xxi therfore god sayth non eris susurro nec criminator populis thou shalt musterer mogis th people lette loue pee ne thou shalt tale teller ne blabbe defame man woman falsly ony synne preui leuitici xixc soche preuy musterers bacbyters make discencion heuinesse euery comonte euery housholde euery cumpany therfore whanne knowe shulde put oute cumpany elles chastised wyse man sayth whane wode withdrawe fyre abateth quenched right sayth withdrawe preuy musterers bacbiters put oute cumpany chidinge debate shal cese prouer xxvic diues ie bilignis thou clepest double tuged man pauper biliguis ye double tuged man say one hys mouwthe thenketh another hys herte sphekethe good byfore man bihynde hym speketh euyl sayth truthe one tyme another tyme forsakethe vnstable speche nowe saythe one nowe another god speketh sayth o bili gue detestor prouerbio rum iiioc iwlate lothe mouthe yt double tunged diues clepethe wyse man thyrd tunge dothe moche woo pauper third tunge ye flaterynge tunge whyche worste euery flaterer flatereth man woman synne flaterer bacbiter double tunged may cleped latey trilinguis treble tunged englisshe flaterer blyndeth folke flaterethe take hede theym sylfe ne god ne knowe thesilfe waye proude yt yeue tale ther euencrysten also flaterer lacketh bacbiteth al tho heteth flatereth plese hi dereth another mannys name enhaunse name maketh discorde discencion also flaterers double tuged lyghtly preysen man woman lightly wyll lacke theym fayle ther purpose haue noo lucre ther flaterige wend haue comonly graete preysers greate lackers moche preyse man woman oute mesure flateringe moch willacke another bacbytinge therfore seneca sayth lauda parce vitupa percius preyse scarsely lacke scarsely skyllis salomon saythe thyrde tunge hathe stired moche ito pride made falle shame shenship dysperpled fro nacion nacion hath destried walled townes dolue vp housis grete forbis hathe kyt weye myght vertue peple ful strong made feble flaterers make townes nacions fordes bolde beginne werrys plees debate whych come nought blent flatering ouer preysinge knowe themsylfe wene ouerlede al men tyl last destroied themsilfe also wyse man seyth thirde tung hath caste stronge wemen saye good wemen syker vertuouse oute ther vertue priued put ther trauayls whane gode woman hath traueyled moch hir lyfe plese god haue gode name cometh false flaterer gyle wyth flatering wordes fayre bihestis matrimony richessys bryngethe hyr synne doth hir lese hir good name bryngeth hyr shame veleny therfore seythe wyse man thesame place eccle xxviiic taketh bede flaterynge tunge thirde tung haue lykinge therin shal neuer haue reste shal haue frende may reste ne trust flaterers true frendys alle blinde men ye thei mai prophetis bihight welth prosite plese people therfore cetye ierusalem destroied nigh al ye cetyes castellys londe hynge sedechie take child slayn byfore hym iyen put oute lordis gentilis londe eyther slayn elles ledde prysoners babyloyne peple sleyn hungur moreyn swerde al tho left lyue cetye ierusalem taken desparpled diuers nacions slayn diuers maner trusted alwey flaterynge false prophetys oure myschefe ayens man precheth nighe al aboute maiten diues sine pauper ofte haue tolde thou beleueste go ouer men shal tel ye thou axe fynde thyrd boke kynges kynge israel who name achab styred prophete al prophetys withe one mouth tel oure lorde kynge good tidynges say yt shal spede right wel praye saye theye saye thanne prophete answered lorde god saythe shal speke oure lorde kynge whanne cam fore kyng said ye king achab sawe bi vison al peple israel despled hillys scatered aboute shepe wythoute shepeherd anon king wrath saide tolde neuer good ne welthe thanne prophete sayde worde god sprite stode forthe sayde shal desseyue hi oure lorde axed hou shuld disseue shal seide go oute aspryte lyer mouth al false prophetys thanne oure lorde god seide thou shalt deseyue hym thou shalt haue wordis therfore wende moche folke wenethe yet criste hadde bode theym haue boughte swerdys feyght therfore answerde maner bygune speke swerdis fightinge thanne crist displesyd wythe ther spech bad stylle spech satis est inoughe suffiseth yt ye haue spoken maner speche nomore mater therfore luke saythe place cesed ther spech anon went crist ito mounte oliuete maner god sayd moyses wha prayde hym might entre londe byheste sufficit tibi inoughe yt thou haste sayde speke nomore thys mater deuto iiioco also god sayde aungel slowe peple sufficit cotine manum tuam inough withold thy honde criste sayd hys dyscyplys tyme hys passion whanne fond slepynge sufficit inoughe ye haue slept nowe awake ye made end slepinge thys worde sufficit suffisethe made ende ther vnkunnyng speche whanne begune speke swerdys thys worde satis e inoughe saye ye haue spoke inoughe mar nomore hereof wyste crist ment nomore tha wyste criste ment wha sayde iudas quod facis fac cecius thou doiste non suche wordys criste vndernam iudas euyl purpose yt shuld amed hi yet custum moch folke yt whane theye ther child seruantys speke vnwysly put silence theym stylle wyth worde say sone inoughe thou hast sayde inoughe diues many clerkys say whanne apostlys sayde lo two swerdys criste sayd ayen satis est inoughe tho wordys crist graunted men holy churche two swerdys bothe goostly swerde bodely swerde pauper theye erre apostlys thei vnderstode whine criste saide tho wordys criste graunted neuyr clerkys bodely swerde shedde blode forbad tyme whanne vndernam peter smiting swerde bad hym put vp hys swerde shethe whi sayth smytethe wythe swerde shall perysshe withe swerde alle processe gospel men vnderstond wel shwethe yt cryste hathe forbode men holy church bodeli swerd therfore saith saint ambrose ther armuer ther fyghtinge shuld bytter teerys holy praiers diues yet contra te criste sayth gospel non veni pacem mittere sed gladium cam saith sende pee erthe swarde mtxco pauper swerde place vnderstod swarde goddys worde saythe glose sward man departed synne wycked cumpanye gospel shewethe wel thys swerde synne slayn mannys soule diues sythe god forbad men holy churche swerde sheddyng blod maslaughter slow sait peter ananyam saphariam hys wyfe hyr false couetouse hir lesinges auctuu vo pauper lawe sayth xxiii q viii petr slowe wythe material swerde power god yaue hi myraclys wythe hys praiers reysed woman deth lyfe who name thabita auctuum ixc wythe wordys hys blamynge toke hir lyfe ananye safira prayde hyr dethe vnder name ther sine non fel doun dede vertue swerde goddys worde petyr vndernam thei repented fende sathanas toke power ouer slowe theim bodely slowe theym fyrste goostly sine false couetyse xxi chapter diues leful oni ca sle oni woma vngylty pauper case lawe deliuer saue hym dethe elles seke sum weye saue shall yeue sentence hys deth pylat traueyled ful besyly saue criste deth wyste vngylty moch cristen iuge oweth trauayle saue innocentys lyf crist bought blode flee false sentence pylat might ought lawe haue saued criste plese peple dred yt shulde haue accused hym emperoure folowed ther wylle put criste deth therfor afterwarde dapned false queste shlat nof ioy ne thyn hond sey false wytnes wycked saye thou shalt make couenaunt saye false wytnesse ne assent therto thou shat folowe peples wyl euyl thinge falsnesse dome thou shalt assent sentence many go aweye truth exo xxiiic therfor lawe biddeth iustice light ne redy leue ne redy take vengeaunce di lxxxvi si quid et xi q viiii quauis et xvi q viii si quid ende euery dome shalbe iusticia bigamie ama shuld haue two wyues gedre ne one woman two husbodis gidre seyd shulde two one flesshe forbad sodomye bnd also wordys sheweth yt eche theim hathe power ouer others body non may conteyne assent theim diues made god woman ribbe ada another boon pauper ribbe nexte hert toke god made hir ny felowe loue helper ribbe nexte herte alboues shulde wyfe next lone al wymen al men god made woman fote mannys thral ne made hir hede mayster hys syde ribbe feolowe loue helper nede wha eue synned thanne woman made suget man wyfe shulde reuled hir husbod drede serue hym felowe loue helper nede nexte solace sorow thral bond vilein seruage husbonde owth haue wyfe reuerece worshyp yt bothe one flessh one blod diues made god woman hirsilfe erthe dyd adam pauper encrease ther loue gedre also yeue woma mater lownesse firste encressyng loue ffor woman part manys body man loue hir owne flessh blod also must loue man hir begynnynge hir flessh hir blode also oweth take grete mtaer lownesse ke yt hir perfection hyr begynnyge haue man reuerence hir perfection hyr pryncipal begynnyg hir firste ordre kynde god made al mankynd one wolde al mankynde shulde one charite cam al one fifte chaptor diues whether auoutre gretter synne man woman pauper comonly synne higher degre ye harder ye fal sinnemore greuous also mor mighty wey ki de withstod hath skyl reson wherby may withstod ware fyndes gyle made maister gouernoure woman gouerne hir vertue kepe hir fro vice falle vice auoutre woman moch blame worthy repreued shamefully therfore saynt austen lio de decem cordis vndernymeth husbodis falin auoutre seyth ech thys maner god seythe ye thou shalt lechery yt sey thou shalt medle withe woman butte wythe thy wyfe thou ayist thy wife medle non therfore thou oughtist byfor thy wyfe vertu thou fallest doue vnder ye filth lechery thou wylt thy wife ou er comer lechery haue maystry fend thou wylt ouercome acowerde ly doue lecherye withstonddynge thou arte hede thy wyfe yet thy wife go bifore ye god thou art hed thy wif goeste bacward hel seyth heed woman therfore housholde woman liueth better ye housholde hangethe hed dounwarde syth man hed woma owethe lyue better woma go byfor wyfe al gode dedys yt may sue hir husbond folow hir hede hede eche housholde husbond wyfe body course kynd theder yt hedde ledethe thyder shulde body folowe wolde thanne hede yt husbond go lecherye wyl yt body hys wyfe folowe wold man go thyder wheder wyl yt wyfe folowe lytyl boke sait austen sayth thus daye day playntes made mannys lecherye al thogh ther wyues dare playn ther husbondys lechery bold customable yt take nowe law moch yt tel wyues yt lecheri auoutry leful wyme thus seith sait auste diues sutyme wist hard ye wyues take lyig wt seruatis brouht court bifore ye iuge moch shame yt husbod brouht court bifor ye iuge laye wt wyme seldo sen pauper yet seyth sait auste ye boke gret sine husbod ye wyfe sudel forsoth saith truth god ye shrewednesse yt maketh le gilty tha woma sine oft take auoutry ne punysshhedd auoutrye wymen le gylty yt thy gylty mighty slygh maynten ther sine nygh eche confortethe synne men witnessys iugis doer punysshe auoutrie woman ouerdone gylty auoutre therfore traueyle nygh al one assent mainteyne ther lecherye woman seldom se voutre therfore ful sclaunderous wha ne fallethe harde punysshed butte men comon yt vnnethys ony sclaunder therof wymen dare speke ayens lecherie men wyl speke repreue lecherye man moche gylty synne seldome falletheis mooste sclaunderous yete case lesse greuous synne ofte falleth mooste vse leeste sclaunderous yet mooste greuous customable blode men synne lesse dreye shame men haue synne greuous ther synne therfore saynt austen place spekethe mater ayens lecherye men sey thus parauenture thy wyfe herethe churche prechynge nott leful take thy wyfe comethe home grutcheth ayes thy lecherye seythe yt thou doeste thynge notte leful criste chastite thou axiste yelde thou owe feythe thou owiste feith owe feyth criste though thou disseyue thou disseyueste god who seruantes bothe thou disseyueste bought v bothe knoweth al weneste thou seyth saynt austen man wylbe heled amend hir wordes nay nay seythe anon shal wroth shalbe wode bothe withe hys wyfe wyth prechoure curse tyme wyfe cam churche truthe wordis seynt austen boke yet boke seyth thus paraueture thou letchoure wolt excuse sey take noon mannys wyfe take myne owne seruaunt wylt thou seythe yt thy wyfe sey take noon husbond take butte seruaunt god forbede thy wyfe shulde sey better haue sorowe thy synne folowe take wycked ensaumple thy wyfe chaste holy woman true cristen woman hath sorowe thy lecherye flessh charite thy wyfe wolde thou doeste amys dothe amys spedeful ye kept hir chast lecherye yt thou shuldeste doo lecherye thou doest lecherye shulde lecherye gode woma kepeth chastitye ye feyth yt owthe butt also seythe owethe criste though man amys yit woman yeuethe hir chaste god therfore saythe saynt auste ye place crist speketh hertys gode wymen wythin ther soule ther husbond hereth worthy conforteth doughter withe suche maner wordys thou art euyl deseased wythe wrongys thy husbonde hath pray ye haue pacience sory lawe saue hir pauper although worthye dye yit hir accuserys people brought hir theder worthy dampne hir ne pursue hir deth gyltye woman therfore seythe gloose place though lawe bid slayne gyltye itt ayens wyl oweth doth thefte sayth clerk athig stolne perissh thoughe theefe haue profyte therby yit boude restitucon yeld gode better tha wha toke boud mak restitucon ye thig fyt cam therof hi ye fyt shuld haue come therof lord tyme ocupied ayens wil haue ameded thing stale may nott axe ayen ne withold expesis shal make restitucion yt thyng worth whanne stale better thefe fre lord couenable tyme place stolen thige lorde wyl receyue thynge mishap perisshe lorde hath non accion ayens thefe lettige restitucon ne fyte might haue come therof fered tyme byfore haue stolen thig bound restitucion thynge also value vse diues man woman bye open markette thyng stolen wening stolen whanne knoweth soth may axe pryse thyng yt owethe withdraw til haue pated hi moch payd therfor pau reymud clerkes sey nay therfore ware another tyme losse also susspeccion theft lightly beggige stolen thig might take thefe nethelesse rightfully axe hys payment hym sold hym whanne hath restored lorde thynge spet thyng ther godys comon may wele make restitucion oute leue consentynge thefte husbond stele thynge wife consent therto haue part therof etige drynkyng vse hir wyll ayens hir wyl may preuely make restitucon ther comon godys doth gyle ne theft hir husbonde doth e aught forbid hir vttrly make restitucion co senting theft siker tha hir obey make restitucion ayens wyl thoughe dyd dedly synne stele thyng hir wyckednesse false couetise people men ben vneue rich sume haue moche litel sume ben riche sume ben pore god hath youen richesse one man dispensacion gouernaunce thanne many yt refreyne wyckednesse false couetise peple wyckednes cause oone man richer thanne nother therfore clepyd riches wyckednesse ne hadde wyckednes adames synne fals couetise mannes herte elles alle men shulde haue euynly riche nowe ben vneuyn richesse synne shrewidnesse therfore godes worlde ben clepyd riches vneuenes wyckednesse iniquitatis id est non equitatis therfore alle riches yt one man hath passinge another riches vneuenesse yat vneuyn eue cristen therfore ben clepyde riches vneuynesse therfore god biddeth riche men yt baillies reues worlde make frendes pore folke bothe yeuig foryeuynge baillie dyd nat harde shuld nat withdrawe tithe pauper hostiensis aunswereth therto saith yat longe synne pryue men shulde nat withdrawe tithe meneth lawe whanne synne ope notorie thanne men shulde nat paie ther soueraigne thus saith hostiensis su sua liiii kubrica de decimis et quare fine allegith many lawes many lawes ben aledgith nat grete clerk gracian decree yt cheif booke lawe canon saithe yt clerke notarie lechour shulde haue part goodes holy churche distinct lxxxi si quis amodo cu aliis caplis sequentibus ther saith glose whome forboden doo office hooly churche forboden interdiit benefice lawe saith al suche notorie lechoures prestes dekenes subdekenes ben forboden office holy chirche yat shulde office holy churche people forboden office therfore benefice forbode til amede hem ibm siqui sunt prisbiteri vpon whiche lawe saith gwydo rosario prestes founde suche open lechoures malefactoures subgettes maye owne auctorite put office natt abide sentence ne doome souereyn al though bisshop wer fauourable suffre suche wycked liuers saith suche suspeded pope lawe diues sentence wonderfulle nat plesaunte men holy church yit thenkith skilful ought dett paied myne enemye strengith malice ayes wyttyng wele shulde robbe therof nat paie dyd moche ayenst robbed cruelly gode thynkith yt paie tithe dueties longe god holy church pore folke paye theym suche wycked lyuers open enemyes god loste euir kept stille paied souerayne hostiensis saith sauf holy churche pore people might holpen therby pauper leful kepe nat ayenst lawe yt aledge ayens hostiesis ayenst clerkes ayenst comon lawe ye lawe acordeth al clerkes wele vnderstonde wordes lawe pretextu nequicie clericorum nequiunt ea decimas nisi quibus de dato diuino debetur suo arbitrio errogare extra libro iii de decimisc tua nobis saye englisshe lewde may nat vnder colour wyckednes clerkes yeue owne tithe butt theym dette comau dement god nat leful yeue awey nother mannes gode withouten wylle lorde goode saith ye lawe wordes nat ayenst hostiense hostiense spekith clerkes open lichours open wycked lyuers lawe spekith clerkes who synne preuy hem defamed falsly malice people biddeth shulde yeuone ayen also lawe saithe shulde natt youen longith commaundement god commaundemente god longe nat suche wycked lyuers therfore shuld nat youen also though lewde man witholde tithe dueties fro suche wycked men holy churche paie likethe yeue away ye wole nat lefulle withoute autorite busshopes busshop hous religion resceiue many tithe parisshe olde custome curat churche may nat lyue honestly bnfice certeyne porcion tithe may nombres x ben made ten bres within x nyne nombre vnparfite alle nombres within x ben vnfite regarde x therfore god bad men shulde yeue tenthe part kepe self nyne partes token al oure parfection cumeth withouten dede makith giltie symony sume thinges ben symonient ben forboden holy churche clerke resigne churche couenaunt shalbe youen neuewe sume kyn suche wylle withouten dede maketh nat man dothe symonye diues wherof came name symonye pau symon magus grete wytche proferyd seint petir grete sume money haue grace holy goste make men hole seknesses wondres make holy goste light men wymen also resceyuyng holy ordre symonye sumtyme side makith order wha sume frend shalbe ordred yeueth bisshop sume yift withoute wityng yat shalbe ordred sumtyme side shalle ordred yeue yiftes bisshopes officer speke may ordred whiche yift busshoppe knowyth nat sumtyme bothe party whan one yeueth takith sumtyme done yitt neither tie frende shalbe ordred yeue hote thing bisshopes officer help cause nether ne bisshop knowith tho yiftes maners may also done symonye yeuynge benefice hooly churche man yeue yift pray may ordryd resceyue benefice ayensey assent natt therto yifte ne biheest ne prayer lettithe nat fro myne ordres ne fro benefice assent therto bifore payng money behighte falle symonye though neuir preuy must resigne myn enemy yeue bihete yiftes mocion wil let symone nat myn assente euery man fauourable hym self owne cause therfore thou shalte haue two assessoures whose counseile thou shalt deme thy self tho shall treuthe reasone take treuthe thou make false excusacion thy synne ne lye thou nat excuse thy self ne accuse thy self falsly ne greuously thyne assessoure reasone wole accorde tho ii wytnesses say thy thought thy conscience suffise nat bere wytnesse ne ful enfourme thy synful lyf take thridde wytnesse thy feyth lete thy doome stonde wytnesse two thre feith saythe thus fides sine operibus mortua est feyth withouten gode werkes dede al though beleue criste man butt thou lyue cristen man elles thou art dede soule worthy die withoute end feith faileth worde thought dede helpith natt blisse anon conscience mynde shal accorde say thus vsith amysse free wyl die skyl withouten remedie sauyng goddes mercy take hede yt thy clergie may nat saue holy wrytt clergie say anima peccatoris morietur soule synner shal dye also thy clergie may nat saue thou dedly synne thou arte bigamus twyes weddyd first crist thy baptym feende assent syn thou art wydowe fro crist weddid another widowe ye feend forsake god pryde weddyd att begynnyng world ne trust thou nat thy dome trauayle flesshe must refrayned fro lustes euyl tacches wha begynneth wexe proude wynsyng kikyng ayenste master yt soule ouir proud rebell maister must haue sharpe bridel sharpe abstinence harde trauayle meke tretable yeue smothe brydel easy abstine ce comyn trauayle raynes thy bridel shulde ii tie temporaunce yt say neither moche ne lytel knyt togidre knot gode discrecion thanne thyne horse shal goo ryghte forthe weye lyf bere heuenly blisse thou yeue thy flesshe moch mete drynke eese wol thy maister flee thou yeue lytel shalbe feble fayle nede let thy iourney sadyl thyn hors shalbe pacience meknesse yt thou paciente aduersite seknesse yt thou folowe nat gruchynges sterynges thy flesshe steroppes thy sadel shulde lownesse sadnes lownesse ayest pride sadnesse ayenst world flesshe thou nat sory wo ne glade wele ne welefare sytt sadly thy sadyl kepe wele thy steroppes pryde ne wrathe seknesse aduersite let nat thy hors cast downe ye sadyl pacience tha syt faste vertue gostly strength kepe thy soule sadel pacience crist byddeth gospel wha saith paciencia vestra possidebitis aias vras ye shal kepe soules paciece sadel maketh horse semely plesaunte sighte pacience maketh plesat sight god men maketh haue loue euery cu pany ben wrath pacience hastynesse maketh vnplesaut withoute loue sadyl god spak caym wha wroth wt brother abel said god art thou wroy thy face thy chere soo falle falle sadyl pacience thou wel thou shalt resceyue goode mede thou euyl anone thy synne cometh att yate punysshed desire syn shalbe vndre thy power horse vndre kniyt thou shalt lorde therof thou wylt gen iiii caym mysgouernaunce horse felle sadyl pacience ito manslaughter brother wolde nat kepe sadyl pacience ne refrayne wycked desire flessh therfore god cursed first al therfore leue freende kepe wele sadyl paciece let angre losse catel ne dethe frendes none aduersite tribulacion seknesse vnsadle pacience sytt ye fast iob dyd say ye sayde whan hadde lost al goode al child slayne self smyten wtth harde sekenesse orrible foule saide thus haue taken goode thinges goddes honde shulde nat suffre wycked thinges peynful soond god yaue god hath taken awaye god wylle done blessyd lordes name iob io et iioc thus syt ye sadly sadel pacience rule ye horse brydel abstinence reynes temaunce horse soo dulle goddes wey pryke ii spore yt drede hel peyne loue god heuene blisse drede loue co pell ye hors hie forth godds wey let nat hors yt flesshe carnalle ease welfare ne feble misfare ouirtrauayle vi chapter master kynde liiiii de qualitate elimetari tellith ther bridde clepyd bernak bridde wexith oute tre ouir water aslong hangith tree dede anon lousith tre fallith downe water anone quykneth swymmeth forth bridde saith hath lytel flesshe lesse blode tree vnderstonde makynde yt came al ada eue tre brauches come al rote bynethe bridde vnderstonde euery woma whiche wha first borne moder dede original synne adam nat able lif grace ne blisse seint poule saith ben alle borne child wrath dethe anone fall fontstone water baptyme ben baptised anon resceyue lyf grace able lyf heuen blysse kepe v besily blode synne carnalite bodye desyres flesshe seint petyr biddeth v abstinete vos carnalibus desideriis que militat aduersus az petri ii absteyne ye flesshely desire fight ayenst soule asmoch iob saith yt al mannes lyf vpon erthe knighthode fightyng ayeste gostly enemyes milicia est vita hois su terra iob vii therfore nedeful euery cristen man gouerne wele horse body haue saide ouir seynt poule saithe must arme gostly armure ayenst dyntes dartes fendes temptacion seint poule saith ad eph vi alle oure fightynge ayenst wycked spirites derknessis whiche prince power gouernoures synful men therfore saithe arme ye armure god ye may withstonde busshemet slightes deuyl stonde fyte al thinges stonde ye saith treuthe gyrde ye lendes wt gyrdel chastite ye habergeon rightfulnesse sheo ye youre foot dightyng gospell pee al thiges take ye shelde feith wt whiche ye may quenche al brennyng dartes wycked feende take ye basynett helth swerde holy gooste yt goddes worde saithe nother place sharper tha ii eggyd swerde ad hebreos iiiio alle maner prayer besechyng pray ye euery tyme alway spirite wake ye alway maner besynesse thus seint poule lyknes bodily armure techith v gostly armure techith v wele arme oure leendes vertue chastite whan byddeth v gyrde wele oure leendes tha byddeth v habergeon rightfulnesse defence body soule yt right al yelde god euery creature yt logith soueraignes felawes subgettes theim bifore v past oute world almesse yeuynge yeldyng dettes ben dede theim ben behynde v cume sauyng right due heritage thus arme v behynde bifore euery syde habergeon rightfulnes right habergeon euery ryng accordeth wt knytt shulde al rightfulnes accord giddre knytt gyddre yt right alle soo man ne woma wronge somoche righte fauoure one yt hyndrynge anothers right tha rynges habergeon rightfulnes accorde nat ne wele knytte togider ther hole wherby feende may hurt oure soule also byddeth v arme foot legges legge harneys yt gostly pouert yt withdrawe oure hertes oure affection erthly thinges nat set loue moche erthely thinges ne worldly godes nat stryue nat plete worldly godes nede copell v therto seke lyue pee wt men may thus arme v gostly pouert oure legges foot say oure loue oure affection ayenst temptacions false couetise therfore byddeth v shoe oure foot dightig gospel pea euery cristen man woman owethe haue gostly pouert crist taughte gospel forther gospel crist gospel pee wyl dede power tech ca nat helpe forther teching gospel goddes lawe helpe gode nedeful sustenauce may haue nede also biddeth v take v shelde feith ye sheld triangle hath thre corner whiche triangle fro myddes drawen thre lynes thre corner ther shulde thre triangle whiche thre one triangle yit none therfore saith feith holy trinyte likned shelde ther thre sone holy trinyte fader sonne holy gooste eche god none theym though ben alle thre one god maiestie sheld feithe holy trinyte v must take v gostly fight bileue hooly trinyte sett alle oure feith alle oure trust one god trinyte pray fadre almighty sede v might sonne al witty graunte v wytt wysdome boly gooste gracious ful mercy graunte v grace may haue miyt wytt grace withstonde al gostly enemyes also byddeth v take v basynett helth saluacion saith glose hope haue maistre oure enemyes helpe god heuene blisse oure mede oure fightynge oure trauayle ther wyl noo man put lauful fight hope haue maistrie mede trauayle basynet wel arayed clene furbusshed rust made slyke smothe shot may sone glide highest al armure goyng gaderyng vpwarde smalle poynte soo muste oure hope oure truste principaly go vp god nat set oure hope ne oure trust moche mannes might ne erthly helpe seint poule biddeth shulde take v rerebras vabras gloues plate say gode occupaciones besynesse gode werkes therfore biddeth v wake al maner besynesse gode werkis wise saith ec xxxiii idelship sluth sorowe care longith ful moche oute prisone ayen welfare butt childe borne myscheyf prisone neuir knowyng better fare yeueth lytel tale ye myscheif prison aslonge hath moder wt sustenaunce though fulfeble maketh sorow ne care logith better fare knowith better moder telle ioye welfare oute prisone sune mone sterres faire floures spryngynge vpon erth briddes syngig myrthe melodye rich arraye lordes lady welth yt oute prison alle hir tale dreme childe bileuyth nat therfore longith nat therafter wole natt al blisse welefare yt spekith forsake modre ne feble fare hath wt bileueth nat yit modre tellith childe child onys prison sawe welthe myrthe welfare whiche moder told wold ful sory wede aye prison lyue wt moder al lyf prison yt firste likinge ynough hi shuld full bytter shulde neuir haue ioye ne rest hert tyl came ayen welefare yt saw prison right thus folke world borne broug forth sorowe care moche trauayle prisone worlde haue moche loue likynge theire erthly moder ther cupany yt say erth erthely thiges erth moder alle yt haue likyng heuenly thinges ne longe nat therafter yit gostly moder holy churche ther gostly fader god hiself fader al tellith blisse heuen butt dreme moders tale childe priso haue sad feith therin though moder holy church tellith v though childe bileue nat yt suche welfare prisone welfare neuir lesse though erthly couetouse haue likig erth erthly thinges bileue nat yt suche blisse heuen yit ther suche blisse neuir lesse fals bileue onys sene assayed lytel blisse ioye likyng yt haue world erthly thinges shuld ful grete bytternes ful sorow care example haue seit petyr criste ledde vpon hylle thabor seynt iohn iames shewid litel blisse manhode face shone bright sune clothes white snowe moyses hely aperyd wt hi grete blisse maiestie tha petir saide lorde ihu lord gode v mak iii tabernacle one ye another moises anoyer hely let v al duel luce ix io sight litel blisse foryat al blis world cared neither mete drik ne clothing hi thought miyt haue lyued withoute ende blisful sight wt cupany also whan seint poule rauysshed heuene hadde seen vision god afterwarde al lif worlde hi peyne moche longyd aye yt blisse therfore saide infelix ego quis liberabit de morte corporis huius ro vii vnsely man shal deliuer fro deth body coueit departed soule body withoute ende wt crist moyses wt god mout synay xl day xl nightes metelesse drynkles fedde speche god p sence yitt sawe butt lytel blisse nat able see blisse ne liuyng worlde god saide hi tyme butt leue frende oure deth kepe wele goddes comaundmentes amende oure mysdedes oure lyf shal see grete blisse neither petir ne poule ne moyses might se erthe shalbe siker blisse withoute ende blisse seint poule saith yt none erthly iye may se ne ere ne hert thi ke ne wytte comphende blisse
